 The limit for foreign investment in government bonds was raised by $ 5 billion to $ 20 billion and the limit for foreign commercial loans was raised to $ 10 billion
 rigerv bank ne kaha ki sarkari pratibhutiyon main nivesh ke liye anivaasee niveshkon kaa aakaar badhaane ke liye sovrain velth fund, multilatural agency, endoment fund, insurance fund, pension fund or videshi kendriya bainkon jaise lambi avadhi niveshkon ko bhi sebi main panjikrut hone kii anumati dene kaa faisla kiya gaya

 pdf The validity and imperative of the Aadhaar card has received another challenge in the Supreme Court
 karnal mathew thomas ne yachika daayar kar court se guhaar lagaai he ki biometric pranali kii kai baar gadabadiyaan saamne ai hai
 Hence its validity is also under doubt
 saath hi har naagarik suvidha or buniyadi adhikaar kii roshni main bhi isaki anivaaryta yachit nahin he
 The Supreme Court has also set the hearing for this petition on Friday
 lekin ummid he ki abaadhar sambandhit sabhi yachikaaon kii sunwaayeesanvidhan peeth hi karegi
 That is, on Friday, the bench of Justice Chelameswar will first combine this petition with the petition filed on Thursday
 iske saath hi donon yachikaaon ko aage kii sunwaayee ke liye samvidhan peeth ko bhej diya jayega
 The petition has also been filed earlier
 
 
 isse pahaleaadhar actako lekar supreme court main buudhvaar ko bhi ek yachika daayar kii gai thi
 The petitioner is a trader of organic farming products, named Nachiket Uduppa
 nachiket uduppa ne apil kii he kiadhar actake tahat sari nijee jaankaree share karne par pabandi lagaai jaae
 Because there is a high probability of misuse of personal information
 durupyog kii sthiti main koi remedial praavdhaan nahin he
 The petitioner has appealed based on the decision of the Supreme Court on the petition of Puttaswamy regarding Aadhar Vs Right to Privacy
 yachikakarta ke anusaar aadhaar ko mobile se link karne ko aichhik yani volentary hi rahane diya jaae
 That is, there is no compulsion to link mobile to Aadhaar
 court is maamle kii sunwaayee bhi isi shuukravaar ko karegaa
 What is Aadhaar Act
 
 
 bataa den ki sarkaar ne kai sarkari yojanaon ke liye aadhaar card ko anivaary kar diya he
 It has been made mandatory for the common man to link the Aadhaar card with his bank account and mobile number as well

 Jammu and Kashmir will be a Union Territory with Legislative Assembly from today
 J-K will be a Union Territory without assembly
 Today is a historic day
 desh kii jananath kahe jane vaale jammu-kashmir or ladakh aaj se centre shasit pradesh ban gaye hai
 After the government of India paralyzed the forces of Article 370 on 5 August, Jammu and Kashmir and Ladakh have become two separate states from today to 31 October
 isi ke saath rajya main sansad ke bane kai kanoon lagu ho sakenge
 Under this, there will be an assembly in Jammu and Kashmir and Ladakh is a union territory
 aaj louh purush sardaar vallabh bhai patel kii jayanti he, jinka jammu-kashmir kaa bharat main vilay karaane main ahm yogadan rahaa
 a gazette (gazette) declaring Jammu and Kashmir and Ladakh as two Union Territories has been issued by the Central Government with the signature of President Ram Nath Kovind
 jammu-kashmir centreshasit pradesh bana he, saath hi saath iskaa punargathan bhi ho gaya he

 What changed the Gazette of India from today to Jammu and Kashmir? 1
 ab tak purna rajya rahaa jammu-kashmir guuruuvaar yani 31 oktober se do alag-alag centre shasit pradeshon main badal gaya
 The area of jammu and Kashmir is separate and the area of ladakh has become two separate union territories
 2
 Under the Jammu and Kashmir State Reorganization Act, Ladakh has now become a union territory without assembly and a union territory including Jammu and Kashmir Legislative Assembly
 3
 Till now, Jammu and Kashmir had the post of Governor but now both Union Territories will have Lt
 Governors
 jammu-kashmir ke liye girish chandra murmu to ladakh ke liye radha krishna maathur ko uparajyapal banaaya gaya he
 4
 abhi donon rajyon kaa ek hi hoicourt hoga lekin donon rajyon ke edwocket general alag honge
 Government employees will have the option to choose either of the two Union Territories
 5
 Most of the central laws were not enforced in the state, now after becoming a union territory, at least 106 central laws will be applicable in both Jammu and Kashmir and Ladakh states
 6
 This includes the Central Human Rights Commission Act, the Right to Information Act, the Enemy Property Act and the law to prevent damage to public property, along with the central government schemes
 7
 At least 7 laws related to land will be changed in the Union Territory of Jammu and Kashmir after the removal of 35-A, which is the right of permanent residents of the state on land and government jobs
 8
 Under the State Reorganization Act, about 153 such laws of Jammu and Kashmir will be abolished which were enacted at the state level
 haalanki 166 kanoon ab bhi donon centre shasit pradeshon main lagu rahenge
 Gazette of India also changes in administrative and political system 9

 pehle cabinet main 24 mantri banaae ja sakate the, ab duusare rajyon kii tarah kul sadsy sankhya ke 10% se zyaada mantri nahin banaae ja sakate hai
